OBJECT Report 11020285 Generic Sales Document
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    Permissions=TableData 7190=rimd;
    CaptionML=[ENU=Generic Sales Document;
               NOR=Generisk salgsdokument;
               SVE=Generellt f”rs„ljningsdokument];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   GLSetup.GET;
                   SalesSetup.GET;
                   CompanyInfo.GET;
                   CompanyInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  IF NOT RequestPageHasBeenShown THEN BEGIN
                     // When saving report as pdf, USEREQUESTPAGE seems to be true.
                     // Therefore the flag RequestPageHasBeenShown is used instead of USEREQUESTPAGE.
                    DetermineDocumentType;
                    InitLogInteraction;
                    // SaveValues is activated. Default values for PDF set.
                    NoOfCopies := 0;
                    PrintSalesLineDiscount := FALSE;
                  END;
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525182;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table36;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document Type,No.)
                                 WHERE(Document Type=FILTER(Invoice|Credit Memo));
               ReqFilterHeadingML=[ENU=Invoice/Credit Memo;
                                   NOR=Faktura/kreditnota;
                                   SVE=Faktura/Kreditnota];
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SkipFillingTempTables THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF (CurrentDocumentType <> CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Invoice") AND
                                  (CurrentDocumentType <> CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Credit Memo")
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));

                               IF CurrentDocumentType = CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Invoice" THEN
                                 "Sales Header".SETRANGE("Document Type", "Sales Header"."Document Type"::Invoice);
                               IF CurrentDocumentType = CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Credit Memo" THEN
                                 "Sales Header".SETRANGE("Document Type", "Sales Header"."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalesReportTextManagement@1100525000 : Codeunit 11012369;
                                BEGIN
                                  SalesReportTextManagement.CreateTextLinesForProFormaInvoiceOrCrMemo("Sales Header", TempSalesReportTextLine);
                                  TempGenericSalesHeader.InsertSalesHeader("Sales Header");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525181;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table37;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempGenericSalesLine.InsertSalesLine("Sales Line");
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525186;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table112;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               ReqFilterHeadingML=[ENU=Posted Invoice;
                                   NOR=Bokf›rt faktura;
                                   SVE=Bokf”rd faktura];
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SkipFillingTempTables THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF CurrentDocumentType <> CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Invoice" THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalesReportTextManagement@1100525001 : Codeunit 11012369;
                                BEGIN
                                  TempGenericSalesHeader.InsertSalesInvoiceHeader("Sales Invoice Header");
                                  IF NOT TempGenericSalesHeader.HasTextLines THEN
                                    SalesReportTextManagement.CreateTextLinesForPostedInvoice("Sales Invoice Header");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525185;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table113;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempGenericSalesLine.InsertSalesInvoiceLine("Sales Invoice Line");
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525184;1;DataItem;SalesInvoiceTextLine;
               DataItemTable=Table11071912;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document Type,Document No.,Document Line No.,Text Line Type,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Document Type=CONST(Posted Invoice));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempSalesReportTextLine := SalesInvoiceTextLine;
                                  TempSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525198;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table114;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               ReqFilterHeadingML=[ENU=Posted Credit Memo;
                                   NOR=Bokf›rt kreditnota;
                                   SVE=Bokf”rd kreditnota];
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SkipFillingTempTables THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF CurrentDocumentType <> CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Credit Memo" THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalesReportTextManagement@1100525000 : Codeunit 11012369;
                                BEGIN
                                  TempGenericSalesHeader.InsertSalesCrMemoHeader("Sales Cr.Memo Header");
                                  IF NOT TempGenericSalesHeader.HasTextLines THEN
                                    SalesReportTextManagement.CreateTextLinesForPostedCrMemo("Sales Cr.Memo Header");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525188;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table115;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempGenericSalesLine.InsertSalesCrMemoLine("Sales Cr.Memo Line");
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525199;1;DataItem;SalesCrMemoTextLine;
               DataItemTable=Table11071912;

                                 WHERE(Document Type=CONST(Posted Credit Memo));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempSalesReportTextLine := SalesCrMemoTextLine;
                                  TempSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
                                END;

    { 1100525062;;DataItem;CompanyInfoPictureLoop;

    { 1100525063;1;Column;CompanyInfoPicture ;
               SourceExpr=CompanyInfo.Picture }

    { 1100525000;;DataItem;GenericSalesHeaderLoop;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               NoOfHeaders@1100525000 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               NoOfHeaders := TempGenericSalesHeader.COUNT;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, NoOfHeaders);
                               IF NoOfHeaders = 0 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               MoveTempSalesReportTextLines;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  I@1100525000 : Integer;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempGenericSalesHeader.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempGenericSalesHeader.NEXT;

                                  WITH TempGenericSalesHeader DO BEGIN
                                    CurrReport.LANGUAGE := Language.GetLanguageID("Language Code");
                                    OnlyReverseChargeVAT := HasOnlyReverseChargeVATLines;

                                    IF RespCenter.GET("Responsibility Center") THEN BEGIN
                                      FormatAddr.RespCenter(CompanyAddr,RespCenter);
                                      CompanyInfo."Phone No." := RespCenter."Phone No.";
                                      CompanyInfo."Fax No." := RespCenter."Fax No.";
                                    END ELSE
                                      FormatAddr.Company(CompanyAddr,CompanyInfo);

                                    CheckDimensionAddress("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");

                                    IF "Currency Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
                                      GLSetup.TESTFIELD("LCY Code");
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                      TotalExclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                      CurrencyCode := GLSetup."LCY Code";
                                      AmountRoundingPrecision := GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,"Currency Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,"Currency Code");
                                      TotalExclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,"Currency Code");
                                      CurrencyCode := "Currency Code";
                                      Currency.GET("Currency Code");
                                      AmountRoundingPrecision := Currency."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END;
                                    FormatAddr.GenericSalesHeaderBillTo(CustAddr,TempGenericSalesHeader);
                                    IF NOT Cust.GET("Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
                                      CLEAR(Cust);

                                    FormatAddr.GenericSalesHeaderShipTo(ShipToAddr,TempGenericSalesHeader);
                                    ShowShippingAddr := "Sell-to Customer No." <> "Bill-to Customer No.";
                                    FOR I := 1 TO ARRAYLEN(ShipToAddr) DO
                                      IF ShipToAddr[I] <> CustAddr[I] THEN
                                        ShowShippingAddr := TRUE;

                                    ShowShippingAddr := FALSE; // not used

                                    IF LogInteraction THEN
                                      IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN
                                        CASE "Document Type" OF
                                          "Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
                                            IF "Bill-to Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                              SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                                4,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Contact,"Bill-to Contact No.","Salesperson Code",
                                                "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'')
                                            ELSE
                                              SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                                4,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Customer,"Bill-to Customer No.","Salesperson Code",
                                                "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'');
                                          "Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
                                            IF "Bill-to Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                              SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                                6,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Contact,"Bill-to Contact No.","Salesperson Code",
                                                "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'')
                                            ELSE
                                              SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                                6,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Customer,"Sell-to Customer No.","Salesperson Code",
                                                "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'');
                                        END;

                                    "Credit Restriction Amount" := AmountIncludingVAT * ("Credit Restriction %" / 100);
                                    CreditRestrictionText := STRSUBSTNO(Text11020254, FORMAT("Credit Restriction %") + '%');

                                    IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice") OR
                                       ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Posted Invoice")
                                    THEN
                                      DocumentIsInvoice := TRUE
                                    ELSE
                                      DocumentIsInvoice := FALSE;

                                    IF NOT RequestPageHasBeenShown THEN BEGIN
                                      PrintLogo :=
                                        (SalesSetup."Logo Position on Documents" <> SalesSetup."Logo Position on Documents"::"No Logo") AND
                                        ("E-Mail (Invoices)" <> '') AND
                                        ("Electronic Invoicing" = TempGenericSalesHeader."Electronic Invoicing"::"E-Mail");
                                      PrintCompanyInformation :=
                                        ("E-Mail (Invoices)" <> '') AND
                                        ("Electronic Invoicing" = TempGenericSalesHeader."Electronic Invoicing"::"E-Mail");
                                    END;

                                    SetFilterOnTempHeaderTextLine;
                                    SetFilterOnTempFooterTextLine;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525057;1;Column;PrintLogo          ;
               SourceExpr=PrintLogo }

    { 1100525007;1;Column;PrintCompanyInformation;
               SourceExpr=PrintCompanyInformation }

               SourceExpr=TempGenericSalesHeader."Specific WKA Percentages" }

               SourceExpr=TempGenericSalesHeader.Amount }

               SourceExpr=OnlyReverseChargeVAT }

               SourceExpr=TextContinued }

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;CopyLoop         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               NoOfLoops@1100525000 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Electronic Invoicing" <> TempGenericSalesHeader."Electronic Invoicing"::"E-Mail" THEN BEGIN
                                 NoOfLoops := ABS(NoOfCopies) + Cust."Invoice Copies" + 1;
                                 NoOfLoops := NoOfLoops + GetPlantLocationInvoiceCopies;
                               END ELSE
                                 NoOfLoops := ABS(NoOfCopies) + 1;
                               IF NoOfLoops <= 0 THEN
                                 NoOfLoops := 1;
                               CopyText := '';
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, NoOfLoops);
                               OutputNo := 1;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number > 1 THEN BEGIN
                                    CopyText := Text003;
                                    OutputNo += 1;
                                  END;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=VAR
                                SalesInvoiceHeader@1100525000 : Record 112;
                                SalesCrMemoHeader@1100525001 : Record 114;
                              BEGIN
                                IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN
                                  CASE TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" OF
                                    TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
                                      BEGIN
                                        SalesInvoiceHeader.INIT;
                                        SalesInvoiceHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(TempGenericSalesHeader);
                                        SalesInvCountPrinted.RUN(SalesInvoiceHeader);
                                        TempGenericSalesHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesInvoiceHeader, FALSE);
                                        TempGenericSalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                      END;
                                    TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
                                      BEGIN
                                        SalesCrMemoHeader.INIT;
                                        SalesCrMemoHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(TempGenericSalesHeader);
                                        SalesCrMemoCountPrinted.RUN(SalesCrMemoHeader);
                                        TempGenericSalesHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(SalesCrMemoHeader, FALSE);
                                        TempGenericSalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                      END;
                                  END;
                              END;
                               }

    { 1100525002;2;DataItem;PageLoop         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1100525025;3;Column;OutputNo_PageLoop  ;
               SourceExpr=OutputNo }

    { 1100525008;3;Column;DocumentCaptionCopyText;
               SourceExpr=DELCHR(DocumentCaption+' '+CopyText, '<>') }

    { 1100525202;3;DataItem;HeaderSalesReportTextLineLoop;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               NoOfTextLines@1100525000 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               NoOfTextLines := TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.COUNT;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, NoOfTextLines);
                               IF NoOfTextLines = 0 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.NEXT;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525212;4;Column;LineNo_HeaderSalesReportTextLine;
               SourceExpr=TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine."Line No." }

    { 1100525092;4;Column;NoOfColumns_HeaderSalesReportTextLine;

    { 1100525079;4;Column;ColumnText1_HeaderSalesReportTextLine;
               SourceExpr=TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.GetColumnText(1) }

               SourceExpr=TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.GetColumnText(2) }

    { 1100525047;4;Column;ColumnText3_HeaderSalesReportTextLine;

    { 1100525110;4;Column;ColumnText4_HeaderSalesReportTextLine;

    { 1100525005;3;DataItem;GenericSalesLineLoop;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               SalesHeader@1100525002 : Record 36;
                               SalesLine@1100525001 : Record 37;
                               NoOfLines@1100525003 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               TempGenericSalesLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type");
                               TempGenericSalesLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
                               TempGenericSalesLine.SETRANGE("Line No.");

                               NoOfLines := TempGenericSalesLine.COUNT;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, NoOfLines);
                               IF NoOfLines = 0 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               WITH TempGenericSalesLine DO BEGIN
                                 VATAmountLine.DELETEALL;
                                 IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice") OR
                                    ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo")
                                 THEN BEGIN
                                   SalesHeader.TRANSFERFIELDS(TempGenericSalesHeader);
                                   SalesLine.CalcVATAmountLines(0,SalesHeader,SalesLine,VATAmountLine);
                                   TotalAmount := VATAmountLine.GetTotalVATBase;
                                   TotalAmountVAT := VATAmountLine.GetTotalVATAmount;
                                   TotalAmountInclVAT := VATAmountLine.GetTotalAmountInclVAT;
                                   TotalPaymentDiscOnVAT :=
                                     VATAmountLine.GetTotalVATDiscount(SalesHeader."Currency Code",SalesHeader."Prices Including VAT");
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                   TotalAmount := 0;
                                   TotalAmountVAT := 0;
                                   TotalAmountInclVAT := 0;
                                   TotalPaymentDiscOnVAT := 0;
                                 END;

                                 SalesShipmentBuffer.RESET;
                                 SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETEALL;
                                 FirstValueEntryNo := 0;
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempGenericSalesLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempGenericSalesLine.NEXT;

                                  WITH TempGenericSalesLine DO BEGIN
                                    SalesReportDetailText := GetDetailSalesReportTextLine(TempGenericSalesLine, TempDetailSalesReportTextLine);
                                    IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Posted Invoice") OR
                                       ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo")
                                    THEN BEGIN
                                      PostedShipmentDate := 0D;
                                      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
                                        PostedShipmentDate := FindPostedShipmentDate;
                                      TotalAmount += Amount;
                                      TotalAmountVAT += "Amount Including VAT" - Amount;
                                      TotalAmountInclVAT += "Amount Including VAT";
                                      TotalPaymentDiscOnVAT += -("Line Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount" - "Amount Including VAT");
                                    END;

                                    IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice") OR
                                       ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo")
                                    THEN BEGIN
                                      IF NOT TempGenericSalesHeader."Prices Including VAT" AND
                                         (TempGenericSalesLine."VAT Calculation Type" = TempGenericSalesLine."VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT")
                                      THEN
                                        TempGenericSalesLine."Line Amount" := 0;

                                      IF NOT TempGenericSalesHeader.Ship THEN
                                         "Qty. to Ship" := 0;
                                       IF NOT TempGenericSalesHeader.Receive THEN
                                         "Return Qty. to Receive" := 0;

                                       IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice") AND ("Shipment No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                         "Quantity Shipped" := Quantity;
                                         "Qty. to Ship" := 0;
                                       END;

                                       IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo") AND ("Return Receipt No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                         "Return Qty. Received" := Quantity;
                                         "Return Qty. to Receive" := 0;
                                       END;

                                       IF TempGenericSalesHeader.Invoice THEN BEGIN
                                         IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo"] THEN
                                           MaxQtyToBeInvoiced := "Return Qty. to Receive" + "Return Qty. Received" - "Quantity Invoiced"
                                         ELSE
                                           MaxQtyToBeInvoiced := "Qty. to Ship" + "Quantity Shipped" - "Quantity Invoiced";
                                         IF ABS("Qty. to Invoice") > ABS(MaxQtyToBeInvoiced) THEN
                                           "Qty. to Invoice" := MaxQtyToBeInvoiced;
                                       END ELSE
                                         "Qty. to Invoice" := 0;
                                    END;

                                    IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Posted Invoice") OR
                                       ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo")
                                    THEN BEGIN
                                      VATAmountLine.INIT;
                                      VATAmountLine."VAT Identifier" := "VAT Identifier";
                                      VATAmountLine."VAT Calculation Type" := "VAT Calculation Type";
                                      VATAmountLine."Tax Group Code" := "Tax Group Code";
                                      VATAmountLine."VAT %" := "VAT %";
                                      VATAmountLine."VAT Base" := Amount;
                                      VATAmountLine."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
                                      VATAmountLine."Line Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                      IF "Allow Invoice Disc." THEN
                                        VATAmountLine."Inv. Disc. Base Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                      VATAmountLine."Invoice Discount Amount" := "Inv. Discount Amount";
                                      VATAmountLine."Reverse Charge VAT" := ("VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT");
                                      VATAmountLine.InsertLine;
                                    END;

                                    SetFilterOnTempBeforeDetailTextLine;
                                    SetFilterOnTempAfterDetailTextLine;
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=GenericSalesHeaderLoop }

    { 1100525035;3;DataItem;VATCounterLCY    ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               CalculatedExchRate@1100525000 : Decimal;
                             BEGIN
                               IF (NOT GLSetup."Print VAT specification in LCY") OR
                                  (TempGenericSalesHeader."Currency Code" = '') OR
                                  (VATAmountLine.COUNT <= 1)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, VATAmountLine.COUNT);

                               IF GLSetup."LCY Code" = '' THEN
                                 VALSpecLCYHeader := Text007 + Text008
                               ELSE
                                 VALSpecLCYHeader := Text007 + FORMAT(GLSetup."LCY Code");

                               CurrExchRate.FindCurrency(0, '', TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date", TempGenericSalesHeader."Currency Code", 1);
                               CalculatedExchRate := ROUND(1 / TempGenericSalesHeader."Currency Factor" * CurrExchRate."Exchange Rate Amount", 0.000001);
                               VALExchRate := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, CalculatedExchRate, CurrExchRate."Exchange Rate Amount");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  VATAmountLine.GetLine(Number);

                                  VALVATBaseLCY := ROUND(VATAmountLine."VAT Base" / TempGenericSalesHeader."Currency Factor");
                                  VALVATAmountLCY := ROUND(VATAmountLine."VAT Amount" / TempGenericSalesHeader."Currency Factor");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525131;4;Column;Number_VATCounterLCY;
               SourceExpr=VATCounterLCY.Number }

      AmountRoundingPrecision@1100525048 : Decimal;
      Text011@1054 : TextConst 'ENU=Sales - Prepmt. Credit Memo %1;NOR=Salg - kreditnota for forskudd %1;SVE=F”rs„ljning - Kreditnota f”r f”rskottsbetalning %1';
      Text11020254@1100525051 : TextConst 'ENU=%1 Credit Restriction;NOR=%1 kredittrestriksjon;SVE=%1 Kreditbegr„nsning';
      VALVATBaseLCY@1100525110 : Decimal;

    PROCEDURE InitLogInteraction@1();
    BEGIN
      CASE CurrentDocumentType OF
        CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Invoice":
          LogInteraction := SegManagement.FindInteractTmplCode(4) <> '';
        CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Credit Memo":
          LogInteraction := SegManagement.FindInteractTmplCode(6) <> '';
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindPostedShipmentDate@6() : Date;
    VAR
      SalesShipmentHeader@1000 : Record 110;
      ReturnReceiptHeader@1100525000 : Record 6660;
      SalesShipmentBuffer2@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 7190;
    BEGIN
      NextEntryNo := 1;
      CASE TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" OF
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesLine."Shipment No." <> '' THEN
              IF SalesShipmentHeader.GET(TempGenericSalesLine."Shipment No.") THEN
                EXIT(SalesShipmentHeader."Posting Date");
            EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
            // Field Order No. does not exist in table Sales Header.
            // Therefore an invoice is handled as a posted invoice with Order No. = ''.
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesLine."Return Receipt No." <> '' THEN
              IF ReturnReceiptHeader.GET(TempGenericSalesLine."Return Receipt No.") THEN
                EXIT(ReturnReceiptHeader."Posting Date");
            EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
            // Field Return Order No. does not exist in table Sales Header.
            // Therefore a credit memo is handled as a posted credit memo with Return Order No. = ''.
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesLine."Shipment No." <> '' THEN
              IF SalesShipmentHeader.GET(TempGenericSalesLine."Shipment No.") THEN
                EXIT(SalesShipmentHeader."Posting Date");
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Order No."='' THEN
              EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesLine."Return Receipt No." <> '' THEN
              IF ReturnReceiptHeader.GET(TempGenericSalesLine."Return Receipt No.") THEN
                EXIT(ReturnReceiptHeader."Posting Date");
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Return Order No." = '' THEN
              EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
          END;
      END;

      CASE TempGenericSalesLine.Type OF
        TempGenericSalesLine.Type::Item:
          GenerateBufferFromValueEntry(TempGenericSalesLine);
        TempGenericSalesLine.Type::"G/L Account",TempGenericSalesLine.Type::Resource,
        TempGenericSalesLine.Type::"Charge (Item)",TempGenericSalesLine.Type::"Fixed Asset":
           GenerateBufferFromShipment(TempGenericSalesLine);
        TempGenericSalesLine.Type::" ":
            EXIT(0D);
      END;

      SalesShipmentBuffer.RESET;
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Document No.",TempGenericSalesLine."Document No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Line No.",TempGenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      IF SalesShipmentBuffer.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        SalesShipmentBuffer2 := SalesShipmentBuffer;
        IF SalesShipmentBuffer.NEXT = 0 THEN BEGIN
          SalesShipmentBuffer.GET(
            SalesShipmentBuffer2."Document No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Line No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Entry No.");
          SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETE;
          EXIT(SalesShipmentBuffer2."Posting Date");
        END ;
        SalesShipmentBuffer.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
        IF SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity <> TempGenericSalesLine.Quantity THEN BEGIN
          SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETEALL;
          EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
        END;
      END ELSE
        EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromValueEntry@2(GenericSalesLine2@1002 : Record 11071889);
    VAR
      ValueEntry@1000 : Record 5802;
      ItemLedgerEntry@1001 : Record 32;
      TotalQuantity@1003 : Decimal;
      Quantity@1004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TotalQuantity := GenericSalesLine2."Quantity (Base)";
      ValueEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.",GenericSalesLine2."Document No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date",TempGenericSalesHeader."Posting Date");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Item Charge No.",'');
      ValueEntry.SETFILTER("Entry No.",'%1..',FirstValueEntryNo);
      IF ValueEntry.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ItemLedgerEntry.GET(ValueEntry."Item Ledger Entry No.") THEN BEGIN
            IF GenericSalesLine2."Qty. per Unit of Measure" <> 0 THEN
              Quantity := ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity" / GenericSalesLine2."Qty. per Unit of Measure"
            ELSE
              Quantity := ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity";
            AddBufferEntry(
              GenericSalesLine2,
              -Quantity,
              ItemLedgerEntry."Posting Date");
            CASE CurrentDocumentType OF
              CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Invoice":
                TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity + ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity";
              CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Credit Memo":
                TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity";
            END;
          END;
          FirstValueEntryNo := ValueEntry."Entry No." + 1;
        UNTIL (ValueEntry.NEXT = 0) OR (TotalQuantity = 0);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromShipment@8(GenericSalesLine@1000 : Record 11071889);
    BEGIN
      CASE CurrentDocumentType OF
        CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Invoice":
          GenerateBufferFromShipmentForInvoice(GenericSalesLine);
        CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Credit Memo":
          GenerateBufferFromShipmentForCrMemo(GenericSalesLine);
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromShipmentForInvoice@1100525016(GenericSalesLine@1000 : Record 11071889);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceHeader@1001 : Record 112;
      SalesInvoiceLine2@1002 : Record 113;
      SalesShipmentHeader@1006 : Record 110;
      SalesShipmentLine@1004 : Record 111;
      TotalQuantity@1003 : Decimal;
      Quantity@1005 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TotalQuantity := 0;
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.");
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETFILTER("No.",'..%1',TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETRANGE("Order No.",TempGenericSalesHeader."Order No.");
      IF SalesInvoiceHeader.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesInvoiceHeader."No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE(Type,GenericSalesLine.Type);
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("No.",GenericSalesLine."No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",GenericSalesLine."Unit of Measure Code");
          IF SalesInvoiceLine2.FIND('-') THEN
            REPEAT
              TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity + SalesInvoiceLine2.Quantity;
            UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine2.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceHeader.NEXT = 0;

      SalesShipmentLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.","Order Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order No.",TempGenericSalesHeader."Order No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE(Type,GenericSalesLine.Type);
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("No.",GenericSalesLine."No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",GenericSalesLine."Unit of Measure Code");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>%1',0);

      IF SalesShipmentLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Get Shipment/Return Rcpt. Used" THEN
            CorrectShipmentForInvoice(SalesShipmentLine);
          IF ABS(SalesShipmentLine.Quantity) <= ABS(TotalQuantity - GenericSalesLine.Quantity) THEN
            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - SalesShipmentLine.Quantity
          ELSE BEGIN
            IF ABS(SalesShipmentLine.Quantity)  > ABS(TotalQuantity) THEN
              SalesShipmentLine.Quantity := TotalQuantity;
            Quantity :=
              SalesShipmentLine.Quantity - (TotalQuantity - GenericSalesLine.Quantity);

            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - SalesShipmentLine.Quantity;
            GenericSalesLine.Quantity := GenericSalesLine.Quantity - Quantity;

            IF SalesShipmentHeader.GET(SalesShipmentLine."Document No.") THEN
              AddBufferEntry(
                GenericSalesLine,
                Quantity,
                SalesShipmentHeader."Posting Date");
          END;
        UNTIL (SalesShipmentLine.NEXT = 0) OR (TotalQuantity = 0);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromShipmentForCrMemo@1100525017(GenericSalesLine@1000 : Record 11071889);
    VAR
      SalesCrMemoHeader@1001 : Record 114;
      SalesCrMemoLine2@1002 : Record 115;
      ReturnReceiptHeader@1006 : Record 6660;
      ReturnReceiptLine@1004 : Record 6661;
      TotalQuantity@1003 : Decimal;
      Quantity@1005 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TotalQuantity := 0;
      SalesCrMemoHeader.SETCURRENTKEY("Return Order No.");
      SalesCrMemoHeader.SETFILTER("No.",'..%1',"Sales Cr.Memo Header"."No.");
      SalesCrMemoHeader.SETRANGE("Return Order No.","Sales Cr.Memo Header"."Return Order No.");
      IF SalesCrMemoHeader.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesCrMemoLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesCrMemoHeader."No.");
          SalesCrMemoLine2.SETRANGE("Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
          SalesCrMemoLine2.SETRANGE(Type,GenericSalesLine.Type);
          SalesCrMemoLine2.SETRANGE("No.",GenericSalesLine."No.");
          SalesCrMemoLine2.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",GenericSalesLine."Unit of Measure Code");
          IF SalesCrMemoLine2.FIND('-') THEN
            REPEAT
              TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity + SalesCrMemoLine2.Quantity;
            UNTIL SalesCrMemoLine2.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL SalesCrMemoHeader.NEXT = 0;

      ReturnReceiptLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Return Order No.","Return Order Line No.");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE("Return Order No.","Sales Cr.Memo Header"."Return Order No.");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE("Return Order Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE("Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE(Type,GenericSalesLine.Type);
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE("No.",GenericSalesLine."No.");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",GenericSalesLine."Unit of Measure Code");
      ReturnReceiptLine.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>%1',0);

      IF ReturnReceiptLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF "Sales Cr.Memo Header"."Get Return Receipt Used" THEN
            CorrectShipmentForCrMemo(ReturnReceiptLine);
          IF ABS(ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity) <= ABS(TotalQuantity - GenericSalesLine.Quantity) THEN
            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity
          ELSE BEGIN
            IF ABS(ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity) > ABS(TotalQuantity) THEN
              ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity := TotalQuantity;
            Quantity :=
              ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity - (TotalQuantity - GenericSalesLine.Quantity);

            GenericSalesLine.Quantity := GenericSalesLine.Quantity - Quantity;
            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity;

            IF ReturnReceiptHeader.GET(ReturnReceiptLine."Document No.") THEN
              AddBufferEntry(
                GenericSalesLine,
                -Quantity,
                ReturnReceiptHeader."Posting Date");
          END;
        UNTIL (ReturnReceiptLine.NEXT = 0) OR (TotalQuantity = 0);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CorrectShipmentForInvoice@7(VAR SalesShipmentLine@1001 : Record 111);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLine@1000 : Record 113;
    BEGIN
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Shipment No.","Shipment Line No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Shipment No.",SalesShipmentLine."Document No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Shipment Line No.",SalesShipmentLine."Line No.");
      IF SalesInvoiceLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesShipmentLine.Quantity := SalesShipmentLine.Quantity - SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity;
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CorrectShipmentForCrMemo@1100525020(VAR ReturnReceiptLine@1001 : Record 6661);
    VAR
      SalesCrMemoLine@1000 : Record 115;
    BEGIN
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Return Receipt No.","Return Receipt Line No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Return Receipt No.",ReturnReceiptLine."Document No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Return Receipt Line No.",ReturnReceiptLine."Line No.");
      IF SalesCrMemoLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity := ReturnReceiptLine.Quantity - SalesCrMemoLine.Quantity;
        UNTIL SalesCrMemoLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddBufferEntry@3(GenericSalesLine@1001 : Record 11071889;QtyOnShipment@1002 : Decimal;PostingDate@1003 : Date);
    BEGIN
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Document No.",GenericSalesLine."Document No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Line No.",GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Posting Date",PostingDate);
      IF SalesShipmentBuffer.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        CASE GenericSalesLine."Document Type" OF
          GenericSalesLine."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
            SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity := SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity + QtyOnShipment;
          GenericSalesLine."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
            SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity := SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity - QtyOnShipment;
        END;
        SalesShipmentBuffer.MODIFY;
        EXIT;
      END;

      WITH SalesShipmentBuffer DO BEGIN
        "Document No." := GenericSalesLine."Document No.";
        "Line No." := GenericSalesLine."Line No.";
        "Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
        Type := GenericSalesLine.Type;
        "No." := GenericSalesLine."No.";
        CASE GenericSalesLine."Document Type" OF
          GenericSalesLine."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
            Quantity := QtyOnShipment;
          GenericSalesLine."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
            Quantity := -QtyOnShipment;
        END;
        "Posting Date" := PostingDate;
        INSERT;
        NextEntryNo := NextEntryNo + 1
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DocumentCaption@4() : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      CASE TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" OF
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Prepayment Invoice/Cr. Memo" THEN
              EXIT(Text010);
            EXIT(Text004);
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Prepayment Invoice/Cr. Memo" THEN
              EXIT(Text010);
            EXIT(Text11012010);
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Prepayment Invoice/Cr. Memo" THEN
              EXIT(Text011);
            EXIT(Text005);
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            IF TempGenericSalesHeader."Prepayment Invoice/Cr. Memo" THEN
              EXIT(Text011);
            EXIT(Text11012011);
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitializeRequest@5(NewNoOfCopies@1000 : Integer;NewShowInternalInfo@1001 : Boolean;NewLogInteraction@1002 : Boolean;DisplayAsmInfo@1003 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      NoOfCopies := NewNoOfCopies;
      //ShowInternalInfo := NewShowInternalInfo;
      LogInteraction := NewLogInteraction;
      //DisplayAssemblyInformation := DisplayAsmInfo; // mboers
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDimensionAddress@1100485005(Dim1Code@1100485003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      Contact@1100485002 : Record 5050;
      DimensionValue@1100485001 : Record 349;
      DimensionManagement@1100485000 : Codeunit 408;
    BEGIN
      IF Dim1Code <> '' THEN BEGIN
        DimensionManagement.GetDimValueRec(1, Dim1Code, DimensionValue, TRUE, '');
        IF DimensionValue."Contact No. (Company)" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          Contact.GET(DimensionValue."Contact No. (Company)");
          FormatAddr.ContactAddr(CompanyAddr, Contact);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPlantLocationInvoiceCopies@1100485000() : Integer;
    VAR
      PlantSetup@1100485000 : Record 11012550;
      PlantLocation@1100485001 : Record 11012554;
      SalesInvoiceLine@1100485002 : Record 113;
      SalesCrMemoLine@1100525000 : Record 115;
      Customer@1100485003 : Record 18;
      FPSLicenseManagement@1100527400 : Codeunit 11229289;
    BEGIN
      IF (NOT TempGenericSalesHeader."Plant Invoice") THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF (NOT FPSLicenseManagement.LicenseAndReadPermissionForTable(PlantSetup)) OR
         (NOT FPSLicenseManagement.LicenseAndReadPermissionForTable(PlantLocation))
      THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF (NOT PlantSetup.GET) THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF PlantSetup."Level One Loc. per Invoice" = PlantSetup."Level One Loc. per Invoice"::Setup THEN BEGIN
        IF (NOT PlantSetup."One Location per Invoice") THEN
          EXIT(0);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF NOT Customer.GET(TempGenericSalesHeader."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
          EXIT(0);
        IF (NOT Customer."One Location per Plant Invoice") THEN
          EXIT(0);
      END;

      CASE TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" OF
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
          BEGIN
            SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
            SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine.Type::" ");
            SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', '');
            IF SalesInvoiceLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF PlantLocation.GET(SalesInvoiceLine."Plant Location") THEN BEGIN
                SalesInvoiceLine.FILTERGROUP(6);
                SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine."Plant Location");
                IF NOT SalesInvoiceLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                  EXIT(PlantLocation."Invoice Copies");
              END;
            END;
          END;
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
            SalesCrMemoLine.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', SalesCrMemoLine.Type::" ");
            SalesCrMemoLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', '');
            IF SalesCrMemoLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF PlantLocation.GET(SalesCrMemoLine."Plant Location") THEN BEGIN
                SalesCrMemoLine.FILTERGROUP(6);
                SalesCrMemoLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', SalesCrMemoLine."Plant Location");
                IF NOT SalesCrMemoLine.FINDFIRST THEN
                  EXIT(PlantLocation."Invoice Copies");
              END;
            END;
          END;
      END;

      EXIT(0);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DetermineDocumentType@1100525008();
    BEGIN
      CurrentDocumentType := TempGenericSalesHeader.DetermineDocumentType(
        "Sales Header", "Sales Invoice Header", "Sales Cr.Memo Header");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetDetailSalesReportTextLine@1100525000(GenericSalesLine@1100525001 : Record 11071889;VAR DetailSalesReportTextLine@1100525002 : TEMPORARY Record 11071912) : Text;
    VAR
      SalesReportTextLine@1100525000 : Record 11071912;
    BEGIN
      DetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", GenericSalesLine."Document Type");
      DetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", GenericSalesLine."Document No.");
      DetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", GenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      DetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Text Line Type", SalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Detail);
      IF DetailSalesReportTextLine.FINDFIRST THEN
        EXIT(DetailSalesReportTextLine.Text);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE MoveTempSalesReportTextLines@1100525007();
    BEGIN
      IF TempSalesReportTextLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CASE TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type" OF
            TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Header:
              BEGIN
                TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine := TempSalesReportTextLine;
                TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
              END;
            TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::"Before Detail":
              BEGIN
                TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine := TempSalesReportTextLine;
                TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
              END;
            TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Detail:
              BEGIN
                TempDetailSalesReportTextLine := TempSalesReportTextLine;
                TempDetailSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
              END;
            TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::"After Detail":
              BEGIN
                TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine := TempSalesReportTextLine;
                TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
              END;
            TempSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Footer:
              BEGIN
                TempFooterSalesReportTextLine := TempSalesReportTextLine;
                TempFooterSalesReportTextLine.INSERT;
              END;
          END;
        UNTIL TempSalesReportTextLine.NEXT = 0;
      TempSalesReportTextLine.DELETEALL;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetFilterOnTempHeaderTextLine@1100525003();
    BEGIN
      TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type");
      TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
      TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", 0);
      TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Text Line Type", TempHeaderSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Header);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetFilterOnTempFooterTextLine@1100525011();
    BEGIN
      TempFooterSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type");
      TempFooterSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesHeader."No.");
      TempFooterSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", 0);
      TempFooterSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Text Line Type", TempFooterSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::Footer);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetFilterOnTempBeforeDetailTextLine@1100525023();
    BEGIN
      TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", TempGenericSalesLine."Document Type");
      TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesLine."Document No.");
      TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", TempGenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Text Line Type", TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::"Before Detail");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetFilterOnTempAfterDetailTextLine@1100525024();
    BEGIN
      TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Type", TempGenericSalesLine."Document Type");
      TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", TempGenericSalesLine."Document No.");
      TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", TempGenericSalesLine."Line No.");
      TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("Text Line Type", TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine."Text Line Type"::"After Detail");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetNoOfBeforeDetailTextLines@1100525012(NoOfColumns@1100525000 : Integer) NoOfLines : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF NoOfColumns = 1 THEN
        TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns", 0, NoOfColumns)
      ELSE
        TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns", NoOfColumns);

      NoOfLines := TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.COUNT;
      TempBeforeDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetNoOfAfterDetailTextLines@1100525014(NoOfColumns@1100525000 : Integer) NoOfLines : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF NoOfColumns = 1 THEN
        TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns", 0, NoOfColumns)
      ELSE
        TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns", NoOfColumns);

      NoOfLines := TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.COUNT;
      TempAfterDetailSalesReportTextLine.SETRANGE("No. of Columns");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetInvoiceCrMemoNoCaption@1100525029() : Text;
    BEGIN
      CASE TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" OF
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice",
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice":
          EXIT(TextInvoiceNo);
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Credit Memo",
        TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Credit Memo":
          EXIT(TextCreditMemoNo);
      END;

      IF (TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" = TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Pro Forma Invoice") OR
         (TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type" = TempGenericSalesHeader."Document Type"::"Posted Invoice")
      THEN
        EXIT(TempGenericSalesHeader.FIELDCAPTION("Due Date"));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetVATAmountText@1100525010(OnlyReverseChargeVAT@1100525000 : Boolean) : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF OnlyReverseChargeVAT THEN
        EXIT(VATAmountLine.FIELDCAPTION("Reverse Charge VAT"));

      EXIT(VATAmountLine.VATAmountText);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDescription@1100409002(GenericSalesLine@1100525000 : Record 11071889) Result : Text[170];
    VAR
      ServiceContract@1100409000 : Record 11012812;
    BEGIN
      Result := GenericSalesLine.Description;

      IF GenericSalesLine."Service Contract No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ServiceContract.GET(GenericSalesLine."Service Contract No.") THEN
        IF GenericSalesLine."Description 2" <> '' THEN
          Result := Result + ', ' + GenericSalesLine."Description 2";
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrice@1100528500(GenericSalesLine@1100528500 : Record 11071889) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF GenericSalesLine."Gross Price" <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(GenericSalesLine."Gross Price" * (1 + GenericSalesLine."Surcharge %"/100))
      ELSE
        EXIT(GenericSalesLine."Unit Price");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetSalesLineDiscount@1100528501(GenericSalesLine@1100528500 : Record 11071889) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF GenericSalesLine."Gross Price" <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(
          100 * (1 -
            (1 - GenericSalesLine."Sales Discount % (Item)" / 100) *
            (1 - GenericSalesLine."Line Discount %" / 100)))
      ELSE
        EXIT(GenericSalesLine."Line Discount %");
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      // TODO KK: Batch post and print does not work fine, because "normal" user filters are "remembered".
      // This issue also occurs in report 206.
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup2 = group2
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object) As Boolean
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function


Shared TransportCostPlusAmount As Decimal
Shared TransportInstallmentAmount As Decimal
Shared TransportPlantAmount As Decimal
Shared TransportRentalUnitAmount As Decimal

Public Function GetTransportCostPlusAmount() As Decimal
    Return TransportCostPlusAmount
End Function

Public Function GetTransportInstallmentAmount() As Decimal
    Return TransportInstallmentAmount
End Function

Public Function GetTransportPlantAmount() As Decimal
    Return TransportPlantAmount
End Function

Public Function GetTransportRentalUnitAmount() As Decimal
    Return TransportRentalUnitAmount
End Function

Public Function SetTransportCostPlusAmount(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        TransportCostPlusAmount = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetTransportInstallmentAmount(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        TransportInstallmentAmount = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetTransportPlantAmount(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        TransportPlantAmount = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetTransportRentalUnitAmount(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        TransportRentalUnitAmount = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function


Shared PageCostPlusAmount As Decimal
Shared PageInstallmentAmount As Decimal
Shared PagePlantAmount As Decimal
Shared PageRentalUnitAmount As Decimal

Public Function GetPageCostPlusAmount() As Decimal
    Return PageCostPlusAmount
End Function

    Return PageInstallmentAmount

    Return PagePlantAmount

    Return PageRentalUnitAmount

    PageCostPlusAmount = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetPageInstallmentAmount(NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    PageInstallmentAmount = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetPagePlantAmount(NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    PagePlantAmount = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetPageRentalUnitAmount(NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    PageRentalUnitAmount = NewData
    Return True
End Function


Shared LinesPrinted As Boolean

Public Function ResetLinesPrinted(PageNo As Integer) As Boolean
    If PageNo = 1 Then
        LinesPrinted = False
    End If
    Return True
End Function

Public Function SetLinesPrinted(NewData As Boolean) As Boolean
    LinesPrinted = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function GetLinesPrinted() As Boolean
    Return LinesPrinted
End Function
